***соответствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствовать.html>соотве́тствовать</a> (2824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соответствовать.html>соотве́тствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sootvétstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> + dative case
</p>
<ol><li>to correspond, to conform, to agree, to comply, to be in line
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цена́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соответствовать.html>соотве́тствует</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́честву</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Cená <b>sootvétstvujet</b> káčestvu továra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The price <b>is in line</b> with the quality of the product.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***соперник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рник</a> (5751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">супьрьникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">supĭrĭnikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sǫ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*perti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat, press up, balk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sopérnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соперница.html>сопе́рница</a></b>)

<li>antagonist</li></ol>

***сопка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопка.html>со́пка</a> (5651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соп</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sop</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mound <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъpъ</i>, related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour, to strew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, meaning "volcano" presumably influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопеть.html>сопе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sopétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wheeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">sopka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">volcano</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">sopka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">volcano</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are borrowings from Russian.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопка.html>со́пка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sópka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопка.html>со́пки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопка.html>со́пки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопка.html>со́пок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>knoll, hill, mound</li>
<li>volcano</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопля.html>со́пли</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sópli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>сопли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soplívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сопли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сопли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snot-nosed, snotty <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with snot running from one's nose</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> young and inexperienced, wet behind the ears</li></ol>

***сопло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопло.html>сопло́</a> (23813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопло.html>сопло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sopló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопло.html>сопла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопло.html>со́пла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопло.html>со́пл</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопеть.html>со́пел</a></b>)
</p>
